<br><font size=-3><font color = white><font color=#009966><a href=?src=[0x30000d5];action=name;character=61c2e56dbcde3b1b2e8722c6686c1381f7b4a4d48e5247b0c8ac74caf77f6b74 style = "text-decoration: none; color: #009966;">Might, Try</a> turned and reached up on the cliff face for any sort of hand hold that would bare his weight even as he slid the fishing rod over his shoulder. He then took a step up, digging the toe of his sandal into the stone face and turning his foot so that he had more surface touching. With a hop he reached another hand-hold and began the systematic climbing of the cliff. He was warmed up now but he was also a little fatigued, so this was just as hard, if not harder, than the first level, and the stakes were much higher. 

Slowly, but surely he worked his way up to the next level. The distance was farther than before but the group was counting on him. Shishorama even cheered for him and let him make the climb first! She trusted him!

The youth winced and hissed as his forearms started to cramp up and his hands went numb with charlie horses but he continued on, stopping only to shake his hands when he felt confident he could hold himself up.

Once Try weakly pulled himself over the top he laid flat on his stomach and took big, gasping breaths for air.

A long moment later the fishing line and scarf were lowered down to the chill boy.</font></font></font>
<br><font size=-3><font color = white><font color=#4a6969><a href=?src=[0x30000d5];action=name;character=b50c547b25a3147f6ec374147486b4aa8928ded90c2d4fbedcfe690c644a296f style = "text-decoration: none; color: #4a6969;">The pale, red-eyed acrobat</a> doesn't grab her on the way up, no. She had been fired off with much too much force to try and slow her down. He could only watch as the pale girl shoots up and over him, to which he turns and waddles in place, determining where she would fall.
